									<h2><span style="color: #000000; font-style: inherit; font-weight: inherit; text-align: var(--text-align);">Why do I love coffee? Oh, there are several reasons.</span></h2><p><span style="color: #000000;">Yes, I just love coffee, and all my friends know it. Just to mention one reason, the whole experience connected to drinking coffee is awesome:</span></p><ul><li><span style="color: #000000;">from the smell when you squeeze the bag in the shop to try to get a whiff of the smell to</span></li><li><span style="color: #000000;">when you open it at home and that strong aromatic scent hits you smack in the face to</span></li><li><span style="color: #000000;">smelling it when it&#8217;s brewing, and then finally&#8230; that long-awaited moment&#8230;</span></li><li><span style="color: #000000;">taking that first sip of the delicious beverage I consider to be liquid gold!</span></li></ul><p><span style="color: #000000;">Who wouldn&#8217;t want to be a part of such an exciting experience!?</span></p><p><span style="color: #000000;">If you&#8217;re like me and just love coffee, you won&#8217;t be able to walk by a new brand of good-looking coffee in the shop without buying it, even if you already have several opened bags at home! (Please comment below so I know I&#8217;m not alone.)</span></p><p><span style="color: #000000;">It doesn&#8217;t matter the time of the day or the temperature outside. But of course, the sound of the coffee brewing in the morning&#8230; is enough to make my day.  When all other sounds seem irritating when you just wake up, this one sound will soothe my soul.</span></p><p><span style="color: #000000;">Yes, I do use the machine quite a bit.  And I know there are other, better ways to brew coffee to get a better taste profile (and we&#8217;ll get back to that later)&#8230; but that sound!</span></p><p><span style="color: #000000;">For the love of coffee &#8211; the sound of coffee brewing in the morning!</span></p><p><span style="color: #000000;">Feel free to browse my website and check out the fun facts in my<span style="text-decoration-line: underline;"> <a style="color: #000000;" href="https://coffee-finders.com/blog/?swcfpc=1" target="_blank" rel="noopener">coffee blog</a></span>!</span></p>								</div>

					<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Smell - what you do before you brew coffee.</h2>				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-df497ab elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="df497ab" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
									<p><span data-preserver-spaces="true">Is there any greater smell than a handful of freshly roasted coffee beans?  I think not.<br /></span></p><p><span data-preserver-spaces="true">You can just smell, smell, smell&#8230; I love it! Then it&#8217;s only one thing to do next. Brew coffee!</span></p><p><span data-preserver-spaces="true">Smell: &#8220;</span><em><span data-preserver-spaces="true">to detect or become aware of as if by the sense of smell&#8221; -Merriam-webster</span></em></p><p><span data-preserver-spaces="true">What a nice way to define the verb to smell. You certainly become aware that coffee is being made, through the sense of smell, when someone is brewing coffee.  And here, where I am at the moment, the smell of coffee permeates the air as the local coffee producers regularly roast their coffee.</span></p><p><span class="navGoBackTitle"><span title="i love the smell of freshly brewed coffee in the morning">I love the smell of freshly brewed coffee in the morning, midday, afternoon&#8230;, basically at any time and on any occasion!</span></span></p>								</div>

					<h3 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">I love coffee so much that I will help you to find new coffee, and enjoy your cup too!</h3>				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-b4e9bcf elementor-widget-divider--view-line elementor-widget elementor-widget-divider" data-id="b4e9bcf" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="divider.default">

						</span>

				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-e8c91be elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="e8c91be" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
					<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">What is this "I love coffee finders" site?</h2>				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-9831da6 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="9831da6" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
									<p><span data-preserver-spaces="true">No, I am not a café, nor do I sell coffee. I just love coffee.  I love good coffee.  And now I like to write about it as well as help others to find it.<br /></span></p><p><span data-preserver-spaces="true">I know there are many out there who love exceptional coffee like me, and there are also some cafeterias named after our common pleasure.  So there are many options to choose from.</span></p><h3>Not Finders Coffee</h3><p>Nope, this is not a misspelling of Finders Coffee. <span data-preserver-spaces="true">The aim of the Coffee-Finders site is to narrow those options to the really good quality ones we (I, and you my readers) have tried and enjoyed.  I love coffee; you my readers love coffee too; and we are coffee-finders because we love to share our experiences when we find good coffee.  </span></p><p><span data-preserver-spaces="true">Thus, the purpose of the &#8216;I love coffee finders&#8217; site.<br /></span></p><h2><span data-preserver-spaces="true">A Little Facts About World Coffee Consumption<br /></span></h2><p><span data-preserver-spaces="true">According to <u>the numbers I found, you can read them under,</u></span><span data-preserver-spaces="true"> </span>20<span data-preserver-spaces="true">21/22 was projected at <strong>176 million bags</strong>.&#8217;<br /></span></p><p><span data-preserver-spaces="true">So, if one bag contains 60Kg of coffee, think about multiplying that by 176 million bags&#8230; that would = &#8230;.  Well, you can do the math, but essentially it means we drink lots of coffee.  The coffee industry is a big business. I have updated some numbers on this in this post </span><span style="color: #3a3a3a;"><b><u><i><a href="https://coffee-finders.com/what-countries-drink-the-most-coffee?swcfpc=1" target="_blank" rel="noopener">what countries drink the most coffee per capita</a>?</i></u></b></span></p><h5>To break down the consumption by categories:</h5><ul><li>According to the <a href="https://www.ncausa.org/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><u>National Coffee Association</u></a>, the most popular types of coffee drinks in the U.S. in 2023 were cappuccino, latte, cold brew, espresso, mocha, macchiato, americano, and flat white.</li><li>The global coffee consumption in 2021/22 was estimated at <a href="https://www.statista.com/statistics/292599/global-coffee-consumption-by-selected-markets/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">nearly 176 million 60kg bags</a>, with the U.S., Brazil, Germany, Japan, and Indonesia being the top five consuming countries.</li><li>The global coffee production in 2021/22 was projected at 168.5 million 60kg bags, with Brazil, Vietnam, Colombia, Indonesia, and Ethiopia being the top five producing countries.</li><li>The average prices for Arabica and Robusta coffee worldwide in 2024 were expected to be 3.86 and 2.51 U.S. dollars per kg, respectively. Here is an interesting article of mine on the topic: <u><a href="https://coffee-finders.com/wholesale-coffee-beans-prices-history?swcfpc=1" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Wholesale Coffee Beans Prices History</a>.</u></li><li>The global revenue of Starbucks, the leading coffee company in the world, reached 32.7 billion U.S. <a style="position: relative; color: inherit; border-bottom: 2px solid transparent; text-decoration-style: dotted; text-decoration-color: var(--cib-color-foreground-neutral-tertiary); text-underline-offset: 3px; text-decoration-line: underline;" href="https://www.statista.com/topics/1248/coffee-market/" target="_blank" rel="noopener" data-citationid="b9b0f30b-f013-adba-240a-36c4440eef28-17-group">dollars in 2022</a>.</li></ul><p>Not to mention <a href="https://coffee-finders.com/coffee-variety-central-america-caribbean/?swcfpc=1" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="text-decoration: underline;">all the good coffee from the Caribbean</span></a>.</p><p> </p>								</div>
		<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-e8b9231 e-flex e-con-boxed e-con e-parent" data-id="e8b9231" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container">
					<div class="e-con-inner">
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-630783d elementor-position-left elementor-vertical-align-top elementor-widget elementor-widget-image-box" data-id="630783d" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="image-box.default">
					<div class="elementor-image-box-wrapper"><figure class="elementor-image-box-img"><img decoding="async" width="1000" height="1500" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%201000%201500'%3E%3C/svg%3E" class="attachment-full size-full wp-image-8215" alt="I love coffee finders Pinterest pin that shows coffee details in a heart shape" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="
						" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://coffee-finders.com/" data-jpibfi-post-title="I love Coffee" data-jpibfi-src="https://coffee-finders.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/I-Love-coffee-pin.jpg" data-lazy-srcset="https://coffee-finders.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/I-Love-coffee-pin.jpg 1000w, https://coffee-finders.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/I-Love-coffee-pin-200x300.jpg 200w, https://coffee-finders.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/I-Love-coffee-pin-683x1024.jpg 683w, https://coffee-finders.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/I-Love-coffee-pin-768x1152.jpg 768w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px" data-lazy-src="https://coffee-finders.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/I-Love-coffee-pin.jpg" /><noscript><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1000" height="1500" src="https://coffee-finders.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/I-Love-coffee-pin.jpg" class="attachment-full size-full wp-image-8215" alt="I love coffee finders Pinterest pin that shows coffee details in a heart shape" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="

I don't only love my coffee for the energy it gives... it's the whole thing. Sharing it, the health benefits, everything.&nbsp; But that's me.&nbsp; So, why should you drink more coffee?</p><p style="font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400">There's no denying that drinking coffee has become an essential part of our daily lives, from the&nbsp;<a href="https://coffee-finders.com/creative-morning-coffee-to-boost-your-day?swcfpc=1" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span>morning coffee</span></a>&nbsp;to the afternoon brew. It's not just a drink anymore; it's a lifestyle choice. What is it that makes it so delicious, and a thing to crave several times a day?</p></p></div></div>				</div>
					</div>
				</div>
		<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-9b195a7 e-flex e-con-boxed e-con e-parent" data-id="9b195a7" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container">
					<div class="e-con-inner">
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-37b16d6 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="37b16d6" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
									<h3 style="font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 400;">Here are a few reasons:</h3><ul style="font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 400;"><li style="font-size: 16px;">If you&#8217;re looking for ways to feel energized and take on the day after you wake up, grab some coffee.</li><li style="font-size: 16px;">There are many health benefits to be derived from extraordinary coffee!  [Check out my <span style="text-decoration: underline;"><a href="https://coffee-finders.com/fun-fact-about-coffee-4-facts-that-will-not-make-you-sleep?swcfpc=1" target="_blank" rel="noopener">post about coffee fun facts here</a></span>]</li><li style="font-size: 16px;"> If you are particular about the taste of things, coffee is great because there is something for almost everyone. Whether you prefer espresso, cappuccino, latte, or mocha, there&#8217;s a cup for almost every taste.</li></ul><p style="font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 400;">Here I will share some tips on how to wake up in the morning and feel like a million bucks. I will also share <a href="https://coffee-finders.com/where-do-coffee-originate-from-part-2?swcfpc=1" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="text-decoration-line: underline;">information about where coffee originates from</span></a>, how it grows, and where to buy it. And I will get into how to roast it, grind it, and brew it.</p><p style="font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 400;">You can buy coffee at the local shop; but if you are looking for something extraordinary for a special occasion, let Coffee-Finders help you.  There are fantastic online options that are easy to order, and are delivered right to your door.  Here are <span style="text-decoration-line: underline;"><a href="https://coffee-finders.com/types-of-coffee-flavors/?swcfpc=1" target="_blank" rel="noopener">some good coffee flavors to try</a></span>: </p><p style="font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 400;"><em>Check out the video under!</em></p>								</div>

							if ( commentParentValue ) {
								url.searchParams.set( 'replytocom', commentParentValue )
